Black Foxes\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Rugby_league" title="Rugby league">\n          Rugby\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/USA_Rugby_League" title="USA Rugby League">\n          USA Rugby League\n         </a>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:2017_Apache_Warrior_400_from_turn_1.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3024" data-file-width="4032" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/2017_Apache_Warrior_400_from_turn_1.jpg/220px-2017_Apache_Warrior_400_from_turn_1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/2017_Apache_Warrior_400_from_turn_1.jpg/330px-2017_Apache_Warrior_400_from_turn_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/2017_Apache_Warrior_400_from_turn_1.jpg/440px-2017_Apache_Warrior_400_from_turn_1.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:2017_Apache_Warrior_400_from_turn_1.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         NASCAR racing at Dover International Speedway\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       As Delaware has no franchises in the major American professional sports leagues, many Delawareans follow either\n       <a href="/wiki/Sports_in_Philadelphia" title="Sports in Philadelphia">\n        Philadelphia\n       </a>\n       or\n       <a href="/wiki/Sports_in_Baltimore" title="Sports in Baltimore">\n        Baltimore\n       </a>\n       teams. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Fightin%27_Blue_Hens_football" title="Delaware Fightin\' Blue Hens football">\n        University of Delaware\'s football team\n       </a>\n       has a large following throughout the state with the\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_State_Hornets_football" title="Delaware State Hornets football">\n        Delaware State University\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Wesley_College_(Delaware)" title="Wesley College (Delaware)">\n        Wesley College\n       </a>\n       teams also enjoying a smaller degree of support.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Delaware is home to\n       <a href="/wiki/Dover_International_Speedway" title="Dover International Speedway">\n        Dover International Speedway\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Dover_Downs" title="Dover Downs">\n        Dover Downs\n       </a>\n       . DIS, also known as the\n       <i>\n        Monster Mile\n       </i>\n       , hosts two\n       <a href="/wiki/NASCAR" title="NASCAR">\n        NASCAR\n       </a>\n       race weekends each year, one in the late spring and one in the early fall. Dover Downs is a popular\n       <a href="/wiki/Harness_racing" title="Harness racing">\n        harness racing\n       </a>\n       facility. It is the only co-located horse and car-racing facility in the nation, with the Dover Downs track located inside the DIS track.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Delaware is represented in\n       <a href="/wiki/USA_Rugby_League" title="USA Rugby League">\n        USA Rugby League\n       </a>\n       by 2015 expansion club, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Black_Foxes" title="Delaware Black Foxes">\n        Delaware Black Foxes\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Delaware has been home to\n       <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling" title="Professional wrestling">\n        professional wrestling\n       </a>\n       outfit\n       <a href="/wiki/Combat_Zone_Wrestling" title="Combat Zone Wrestling">\n        Combat Zone Wrestling\n       </a>\n       (CZW). CZW has been affiliated with the annual Tournament of Death and\n       <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_Wrestling_Association" title="East Coast Wrestling Association">\n        ECWA\n       </a>\n       with its annual\n       <a href="/wiki/ECWA_Super_8_Tournament" title="ECWA Super 8 Tournament">\n        Super 8 Tournament\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Delaware\'s official state sport is\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bicycling" title="Bicycling">\n        bicycling\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96">\n        <a href="#cite_note-96">\n         [94]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Delaware_Native_Americans">\n        Delaware Native Americans\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       Delaware is also the name of a Native American group (called in their own language\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lenni_Lenape" title="Lenni Lenape">\n        Lenni Lenape\n       </a>\n       ) that was influential in the colonial period of the United States and is today headquartered in Cheswold, Kent County, Delaware. A band of the Nanticoke tribe of American Indians today resides in Sussex County and is headquartered in Millsboro, Sussex County, Delaware.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Namesakes">\n        Namesakes\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        Several ships have been named\n        <a href="/wiki/USS_Delaware" title="USS Delaware">\n         USS\n         <i>\n          Delaware\n         </i>\n        </a>\n        in honor of this state.\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Delawareans">\n        Delawareans\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_people_from_Delaware" title="List of people from Delaware">\n        List of people from Delaware\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">\n        See also\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n class="mw-cite-backlink">\n           <b>\n            <a href="#cite_ref-WhichRegion_10-0">\n             ^\n            </a>\n           </b>\n          </span>\n          <span class="reference-text">\n           While the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Census_Bureau" title="U.S. Census Bureau">\n            U.S. Census Bureau\n           </a>\n           designates Delaware as one of the\n           <a href="/wiki/South_Atlantic_States" title="South Atlantic States">\n            South Atlantic States\n           </a>\n           , it is usually grouped with the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mid-Atlantic_States" title="Mid-Atlantic States">\n            Mid-Atlantic States\n           </a>\n           or the\n           <a <span class="reference-text">\n           Because of surveying errors, the actual line is several compound arcs with centers at different points in New Castle.\n          </span>\n         </li>\n C. Scribner\'s Sons. p.\xc2\xa08.\n          </cite>\n          <span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ADelaware&amp;rft.au=Myers%2C+Albert+Cook&amp;rft.btitle=Narratives+of+Early+Pennsylvania%2C+West+New+Jersey+and+Delaware%2C+1630%E2%80%931707%2C+Volume+13&amp;rft.date=1912&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.pages=8&amp;rft.pub=C.+Scribner%27s+Sons&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook">\n           <span style="display:none;">\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </span>\n        </li>\n        <li id="cite_note-13">\n         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">\n          <b>\n           <a href="#cite_ref-13">\n            ^\n           </a>\n          </b>\n         </span>\n         <span class="reference-text">\n          "The First to Ratify" would be more accurate, as the beginnings of the states themselves date back to the Declaration of Independence, celebrated July 4, 1776, when what was to become the State of Delaware was still the three lower counties of Pennsylvania with the governor in Philadelphia, and not establishing independence from that body until\n          <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Constitution_of_1776#Background" title="Delaware Constitution of 1776">\n           September 20, 1776\n          </a>\n          . According to Delaware\'s own website, "Delaware became a state in 1776, just two months after the signing of the Declaration of Independence." (ref-\n          <a class="external text" href="http://delaware.gov/facts/DelawareFactsandSymbols.pdf" rel="nofollow">\n           pdf\n          </a>\n          ) Therefore Delaware was actually the\n          <i>\n           last\n          </i>\n          of the thirteen colonies to establish itself as a state. Additionally, the\n          <a href="/wiki/50_State_Quarters#Designs" title="50 State Quarters">\n           Delaware State Quarter\n          </a>\n          is minted with this nickname, yet shows\n          <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Rodney#American_Revolution" title="Caesar Rodney">\n           Caesar Rodney\n          </a>\n          on horseback in commemoration of how he was the\n          <i>\n           last\n          </i>\n          delegate to show up to the Continental Congress for the historic vote for independence. And with regard to the original Articles of Confederation, Delaware was the\n          <a href="/wiki/Articles_of_Confederation#Ratification" title="Articles of Confederation">\n           12th of the 13 states to ratify\n          </a>\n          .\n         </span>\n        </li>\n        <li id="cite_note-14">\n         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">\n          <b>\n           <a href="#cite_ref-14">\n            ^\n           </a>\n          </b>\n         </span>\n         <span class="reference-text">\n          <cite class="citation book">\n           Ware DeGidio, Wanda (2011).
